## <a name="onedrive-for-business-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-1914">Funzionalità di OneDrive for Business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1914">OneDrive for Business features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1915">OneDrive for business (in precedenza SkyDrive Pro) è uno spazio di archiviazione online personale nel cloud.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1915">OneDrive for Business (formerly SkyDrive Pro) is personal online storage space in the cloud.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1916">Utilizzarla per archiviare i file di lavoro su più dispositivi con facilità e sicurezza.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1916">Use it to store your work files across multiple devices with ease and security.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1917">Condividere i file con i colleghi in base alle esigenze e modificare i documenti di Office insieme in tempo reale con Office per il Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1917">Share your files with colleagues as needed, and edit Office documents together in real time with Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1918">Sincronizzare i file nel computer locale utilizzando l'app di sincronizzazione di OneDrive for business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1918">Sync files to your local computer using the OneDrive for Business sync app.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1919">OneDrive for Business è incluso in SharePoint Online, ma può essere acquistato anche come piano autonomo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1919">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online and can also be purchased as a standalone plan.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1920">L'opzione autonoma di OneDrive for business include Office per il Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1920">The OneDrive for Business standalone option includes Office for the web.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1921">Per ulteriori informazioni, vedere [che cos'è OneDrive for business?](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1921">To learn more, see [What is OneDrive for Business?](https://support.office.com/article/187f90af-056f-47c0-9656-cc0ddca7fdc2?ocmsassetID=HA102822076).</span></span>
  
### <a name="system-requirements"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-1922">Requisiti di sistema</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1922">System Requirements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1923">Il client di sincronizzazione di OneDrive for business ha diversi requisiti di sistema rispetto al client di OneDrive.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1923">The OneDrive for Business sync client has different system requirements than the OneDrive client.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1924">Per ulteriori informazioni, vedere [come installare il client di sincronizzazione di OneDrive for business](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1924">To learn more, see [How to install the OneDrive for Business sync client](https://support2.microsoft.com/kb/2903984).</span></span>
  
### <a name="onedrive-for-business-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-1925">Limiti di OneDrive for business</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1925">OneDrive for Business limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1926">OneDrive for business piano 1 fornisce 1 TB di spazio di archiviazione per utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1926">OneDrive for Business Plan 1 provides 1 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1927">I seguenti piani di qualificazione forniscono un'archiviazione OneDrive illimitata per utente per gli abbonamenti con almeno cinque utenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1927">The following qualifying plans provide unlimited OneDrive storage per user for subscriptions with at least five users.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1928">Microsoft fornirà un iniziale 5 TB di spazio di archiviazione per utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1928">Microsoft will provide an initial 5 TB of storage space per user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1929">I clienti che desiderano un'ulteriore archiviazione di OneDrive possono richiederla se necessario contattando il supporto tecnico Microsoft.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1929">Customers who want additional OneDrive storage can request it as needed by contacting Microsoft Support.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1930">Gli abbonamenti con meno di cinque utenti ricevono 1 TB di spazio di archiviazione per utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1930">Subscriptions with less than five users receive 1 TB of storage per user.</span></span>
  
- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1931">Office 365 A1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1931">Office 365 A1</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1932">Office 365 A3</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1932">Office 365 A3</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1933">Office 365 A5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1933">Office 365 A5</span></span>
    
<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1934">Non è possibile allocare altro spazio di archiviazione a un utente di OneDrive specifico.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1934">You cannot allocate more storage to a specific OneDrive user.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1935">Tuttavia, è possibile abbassare la quantità di spazio di archiviazione visualizzato da un utente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1935">However, you can lower the amount of storage that a user sees.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1936">Se un utente di Office 365 Enterprise F1 ha bisogno di più spazio di archiviazione, sarà necessario eseguire l'aggiornamento a Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1936">If an Office 365 Enterprise F1 user needs more storage, then you'll need to upgrade to Office 365 Enterprise E1.</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1937">Per informazioni sui tipi di file che non è possibile aggiungere a OneDrive for business, vedere [tipi di file che non possono essere aggiunti a un elenco o a una raccolta](https://support.office.com/article/30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1937">For information about file types that you can't add to OneDrive for Business, see [Types of files that cannot be added to a list or library](https://support.office.com/article/30be234d-e551-4c2a-8de8-f8546ffbf5b3).</span></span>
  
<span data-ttu-id="9928a-1938">OneDrive for Business è compreso in SharePoint Online.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1938">OneDrive for Business is included in SharePoint Online.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-1939">Per ulteriori informazioni sulle limitazioni in SharePoint Online, ad esempio le quote di raccolta siti, i limiti di caricamento dei file e i limiti di archiviazione, vedere [frontiere e limiti del software di SharePoint Online](../sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-1939">To learn about additional limitations in SharePoint Online, such as site collection quotas, file upload limits, and storage limits, see [SharePoint Online software boundaries and limits](../sharepoint-online-service-description/sharepoint-online-limits.md).</span></span>

and compliance features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3450">A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span ### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-3454">Limiti di Skype for business online</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3454">Skype for Business Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3455">I limiti di Skype for business online rientrano nelle categorie seguenti:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3455">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3456">Limiti peer-to-peer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3456">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3457">Limiti delle riunioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3457">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3458">Limiti di conservazione delle riunioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3458">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3459">Limiti di minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3459">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9928a-p219">I limiti applicati a un'organizzazione di Office 365 potrebbero variare in base al tempo di registrazione dell'organizzazione nel servizio. Quando un limite viene modificato nei datacenter Microsoft, la modifica può richiedere un certo tempo per essere applicata a tutti i clienti esistenti.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-p219">The limits applied to an Office 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service. When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-3462">Limiti peer-to-peer</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3462">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-p220">**Limite di trasferimento file** La dimensione massima relativa a un file che può essere trasferito in una conversazione di messaggistica istantanea di Skype for Business online. Per informazioni sui tipi di file per i quali è stato bloccato il trasferimento file, vedere l'articolo del supporto Microsoft relativo all' [invio e ricezione di file o allegati in Skype for Business Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-p220">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3465">**Limiti relativi alle conversazioni a schede aperte** Il numero massimo di schede di conversazione che gli utenti di Skype for Business possono aprire in contemporanea.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3465">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>

#### <a name="meeting-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-3478">Limiti delle riunioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3478">Meeting limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3479">**Limite caricamento file** La dimensione massima relativa ai file che possono essere caricati durante una riunione in Skype for Business, inclusi gli stampati e le presentazioni PowerPoint.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3479">**File upload limit** The maximum size of files that can be uploaded to a Skype for Business meeting, including handouts and PowerPoint presentations.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3480">**Partecipanti a una riunione in Skype for Business** Il numero massimo di partecipanti (compreso il relatore) che possono prendere parte a una singola riunione in Skype for Business.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3480">**Participants in a Skype for Business meeting** The maximum number of participants (including the presenter) who can join a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3483">**Partecipanti anonimi in Skype for Business Web App** Il numero massimo di partecipanti alla riunione in Skype for Business Web App che possono prendervi parte in modo autonomo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3483">**Skype for Business web app anonymous participants** The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can anonymously join a meeting.</span></span>

The full participant list remains visible to the presenters in the meeting. Also, Gallery View and IM errors are hidden from the attendees.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-3520">Limiti di conservazione delle riunioni</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3520">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9928a-3522">**Periodo di scadenza della riunione** La quantità di tempo dopo la quale una riunione è terminata in cui l'utente può accedere alla riunione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3522">**Meeting expiration period** The amount of time after a meeting has ended that users can access the meeting.</span></span>

#### <a name="minute-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9928a-3552">Limiti di minuti</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3552">Minute limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9928a-3553">Per informazioni sulle limitazioni dei minuti nei piani per chiamate nazionali e internazionali in Skype for business online, vedere [termini di utilizzo dei servizi PSTN di Skype for business online](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoftteams/complimentary-dial-out-period#skype-for-business-pstn-services).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9928a-3553">For information about minute limitations in Skype for Business Online Domestic and International Calling Plans, see [Skype for Business Online PSTN services use terms](https://docs.microsoft.com/microsoftteams/complimentary-dial-out-period#skype-for-business-pstn-services).</span></span>
